In [172]:
train = []
for species_id, species in enumerate(plants_species):
    for file in os.listdir(os.path.join(train_dir, species)):
        train.append(['C:/Users/aksha/Desktop/PLANT_SEEDLINGS/train/{}/{}'.format(species,file), species_id, species])
        train_df = pd.DataFrame(train, columns=['filepath', 'species_id', 'species'])
#print('train_df.shape = ', train_df.shape)
